(the &#8220;Company&#8221;) issued a press release announcing its financial results for the third quarter ended September&#160;30, 2021. A copy of the press release is attached hereto as Exhibit&#160;99.1. </p> <p style="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; text-indent:4%; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">The information in this Item and the exhibit attached hereto are being furnished and shall not be deemed &#8220;filed&#8221; for the purposes of Section&#160;18 of the Securities Exchange Act of 1934, as amended (the &#8220;Exchange Act&#8221;), or otherwise subject to the liabilities of that section, nor shall they be deemed incorporated by reference into any filing under the Exchange Act or the Securities Act of 1933, as amended, whether filed before or after the date hereof and regardless of any general incorporation language in such filing. </p> <p style="font-size:18pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&#160;</p>

 <BODY BGCOLOR="WHITE">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="right"><B>Exhibit 99.1 </B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g200650g57l90.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>Silverback Therapeutics Reports Third Quarter 2021 Financial Results and Provides Business Update
</B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>SEATTLE &#150; November</B><B></B><B>&nbsp;10, 2021</B> <B>&#150; </B>Silverback Therapeutics, Inc. (Nasdaq: SBTX) (&#147;Silverback&#148;), a
clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company leveraging its proprietary ImmunoTAC technology platform to develop systemically delivered, tissue targeted therapeutics for the treatment of cancer, chronic viral infections, and other serious diseases,
today reported financial results for the third quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 and provided a business update. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">&#147;In the third quarter, we
provided our first interim clinical update for the dose escalation arms of the <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">SBT6050-101</FONT> trial, establishing <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">proof-of-mechanism</FONT></FONT>
for SBT6050 as evidenced by the activation of the innate and adaptive immune system in patients,&#148; said Laura Shawver, Ph.D., chief executive officer of Silverback. &#147;In a short period of time, we have accumulated a robust clinical data set
that has informed our development strategy. We are focused on advancing SBT6050 in patients with HER2-expressing cancers such as gastroesophageal and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-small</FONT> cell lung, in combination with agents that we
believe will maximize the therapeutic potential of our <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">first-in-class</FONT></FONT> TLR8 agonist conjugate. We also look forward to continuing to advance our pipeline, including
SBT6290 for patients with bladder, triple negative breast, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-small</FONT> cell lung, and head&nbsp;&amp; neck cancers, and SBT8230 for patients with chronic hepatitis B virus.&#148; </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>Recent Business Updates: </I></B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>SBT6050 <FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(HER2-TL8</FONT> ImmunoTAC) </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B><I>Interim clinical data presented at the European Society for Medical Oncology (ESMO) 2021 Annual Meeting.
</I></B>In September 2021, Silverback presented interim clinical results from the ongoing Phase 1/1b study of SBT6050, including data that establish <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">proof-of-mechanism</FONT></FONT>
through SBT6050&#146;s ability to activate myeloid, T and NK cells, as well as evidence of SBT6050 payload localization in the tumor microenvironment. Adverse events reported were consistent with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">on-mechanism</FONT>
immune activation, and early signals of anti-tumor activity were observed. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B><I>Selected go forward dose of 0.3 mg/kg SBT6050 in combination with <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap"><FONT
STYLE="white-space:nowrap">anti-PD-1</FONT></FONT> therapy in expansion cohorts. </I></B>Silverback is prioritizing combination with Libtayo in gastroesophageal and <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-small</FONT> cell lung cancers and plans to
initiate these expansion cohorts in the fourth quarter of 2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B><I>SBT6050 expanded clinical development strategy announced, leveraging combination with
trastuzumab-containing regimens.</I></B> In the first quarter of 2022, Silverback plans to initiate <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">SBT6050-201,</FONT> a Phase 1/2 study of SBT6050 combined with Enhertu, or with Herceptin and Tukysa with or without
capecitabine, in patients with HER2-expressing or HER2-amplified cancers. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>SBT6290
<FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">(Nectin4-TL8</FONT> ImmunoTAC) </I></B></P> <P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B><I>SBT6290 Investigational New Drug application submitted to the U.S. Food and Drug Administration.
</I></B>Silverback remains on track to initiate the phase 1/1b trial in the first quarter of 2022, and plans to enroll patients with bladder, <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-small</FONT> cell lung, triple negative breast, and head and neck
cancers in dose escalation. </P></TD></TR></TABLE> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B><I>SBT8230 (ASGR1-TLR8 ImmunoTAC for chronic HBV) </I></B></P>
<P STYLE="font-size:6pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>
<TABLE STYLE="BORDER-COLLAPSE:COLLAPSE; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt" BORDER="0" CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" WIDTH="100%">
<TR style = "page-break-inside:avoid">
<TD WIDTH="5%">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="3%" VALIGN="top" ALIGN="left">&#149;</TD>
<TD WIDTH="1%" VALIGN="top">&nbsp;</TD>
<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P ALIGN="left" STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-family:Times New Roman; font-size:10pt"><B><I>SBT8230 preclinical development continues with GLP toxicology studies expected to commence in the first
quarter of 2022. </I></B>Silverback will be providing a preclinical update on the SBT8230 program at the American Association for the Study of Liver Diseases (AASLD) 2021 conference held from November <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">12-14,</FONT>
2021. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
</DIV></Center>


<p style="margin-top:1em; margin-bottom:0em; page-break-before:always">
<HR SIZE="3" style="COLOR:#999999" WIDTH="100%" ALIGN="CENTER">


<Center><DIV STYLE="width:8.5in" align="left">

 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt" ALIGN="center">


<IMG SRC="g200650g57l90.jpg" ALT="LOGO">
 </P> <p STYLE="margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt ; font-size:8pt">&nbsp;</P>
 <P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>Third Quarter Financial Results </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">For the third quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2021, Silverback reported a net loss of $22.7&nbsp;million, compared to a net loss of $8.1&nbsp;million for the
comparable period in 2020. For the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2021, Silverback reported a net loss of $66.0&nbsp;million, compared to a net loss of $19.9&nbsp;million for the comparable period in 2020. Included in the net losses for the
three and nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 were $5.0&nbsp;million and $14.0&nbsp;million of <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">non-cash</FONT> stock-based compensation, respectively, compared to $0.2&nbsp;million and $0.4&nbsp;million for the
same periods in 2020, respectively. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Research and development expenses for the third quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 were $15.6&nbsp;million,
compared to $6.2&nbsp;million for the same period in 2020. Research and development expenses for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 were $45.6&nbsp;million compared to $15.7&nbsp;million for the same period in 2020. The increases in the
Company&#146;s research and development expenses in 2021 were primarily attributable to the advancement of pipeline programs, including SBT6290 and SBT8230, through preclinical development and the continued clinical development of SBT6050.
Silverback also incurred additional personnel-related expenses as operations grew in support of program advancements. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">General and administrative expenses
for the third quarter ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 were $7.0&nbsp;million, compared to $1.9&nbsp;million for the same period in 2020. General and administrative expenses for the nine months ended September&nbsp;30, 2021 were $20.4&nbsp;million,
compared to $4.1&nbsp;million for the same period in 2020. The increases in general and administrative expenses were primarily attributable to an increase in personnel-related expenses due to increased headcount in 2021, including new executives, as
well as increases in salaries, bonuses, and stock-based compensation. The increases in general and administrative expenses were also due to an increase in legal fees, professional fees, and other various general and administrative expenses as we now
operate as a public company. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">As of September&nbsp;30, 2021, Silverback reported cash, cash equivalents, and investments of $340.6&nbsp;million compared
to cash and cash equivalents of $386.6&nbsp;million at December&nbsp;31, 2020, which is expected to fund operating expenses and capital expenditure requirements into 2024. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:18pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman"><B>About&nbsp;Silverback Therapeutics </B></P> <P STYLE="margin-top:6pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Silverback
Therapeutics, Inc.&nbsp;is a clinical-stage biopharmaceutical company focused on leveraging its proprietary ImmunoTAC technology platform to develop systemically delivered and tissue targeted therapeutics for the treatment of cancer, chronic viral
infections, and other serious diseases. Silverback&#146;s platform enables the strategic pairing of proprietary payloads that modulate key disease modifying pathways with monoclonal antibodies directed at specific disease sites. Initially,
Silverback is creating a new class of targeted immuno-oncology agents that direct a TLR8 agonist myeloid cell activator to the tumor microenvironment in solid tumors to promote cancer cell killing.&nbsp;Silverback Therapeutics&nbsp;is located
in&nbsp;Seattle, Washington. To learn more, visit&nbsp;<U>www.silverbacktx.com</U>. </P>
</DIV></Center>

e.removeAttribute('id');a.parentNode.appendChild(e)}}
if(e)e.style.display='block';Show.LastAR=e};Show.hideAR=function(){Show.LastAR.style.display='none'};Show.toggleNext=function(a){var e=a;while(e.nodeName!='DIV')e=e.nextSibling;if(!e.style){}else if(!e.style.display){}else{var d,p_;if(e.style.display=='none'){d='block';p='-'}else{d='none';p='+'}
